class="details-section description simple contains-text-link"> <div class="details-section-contents show-more-container" data-show-use-buffer="true">  <div class="heading"> Description </div> <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description"> <div class="id-app-orig-desc">Welcome to the glamorous world of My Talking Angela! Adopt Angela as your very own virtual pet and give her a fabulous life! She’s all yours to look after from kitten to cat.<p>Dress up Angela in the latest fashions and the cutest costumes and give her the most amazing hairstyles. Make her home beautiful and feed her delicious treats. Just watch – she’ll become your new best friend! You can play games together, collect cool stickers to trade with your friends, and just have loads of fun. Make Angela your very own superstar!<p>- NURTURE YOUR ANGELA: Adopt Angela as a cute kitten and help her grow into a stylish city kitty. From teeth brushing to clothes shopping – she’s all yours!<br>- EXPRESS YOUR CREATIVITY: You’re fabulous so make Angela fabulous too! Upgrade and personalize her home and wardrobe in loads of different ways. Make it look exactly the way you want! <br>- PLAY DRESS UP: Let your stunning sense of style shine through and dress up Angela in the latest fashions and the cutest accessories. <br>- PLAY GAMES: Discover and play amazing new mini games! <br>- COLLECT STICKERS: Find and collect hundreds of virtual stickers, each decorated with brand new images of Angela, and place them in your own super special album. You can even trade the stickers with other players to complete your album.<br>- GET EXCLUSIVE CLOTHES: Make Angela sparkle in amazing outfits by collecting special stickers and unlocking exclusive new clothes.<br>- PLAY WITH ANGELA: Angela has life-like emotions so be nice! Engage with her on screen and watch how she responds. You can talk and sing to her and she’ll repeat everything!<p>This app is PRIVO certified. The PRIVO safe harbor seal indicates Outfit7 has established COPPA compliant privacy practices to protect your child’s personal information. Our apps do not allow younger children to share their information.<p>This app contains:<br>- Promotion of Outfit7&#39;s products and contextual advertising<br>- Links that direct users to other apps and Outfit7&#39;s websites<br>- Personalization of content to entice users to play the app again<br>- The possibility to use and connect with friends via social networks<br>- Watching videos of Outfit7&#39;s animated characters via You Tube integration<br>- Items are available for different prices in virtual currency, depending on the current level reached by the player<br>- Alternative options to access all functionalities of the app without making any in-app purchase using real money (level progress, games, in-game functionalities, ads)<p>Terms of use: <a target="_blank">http://outfit7.com/eula-android/</a><br>Privacy policy: <a With this tiger cat you can do that. What is more, you can enjoy cat games and talking cat friends wherever you are, for as long as you want, because this tomcat Toby is portable and it is a talking cat that repeats what you say! The app is simple, which is why it&#39;s a good cat game for toddlers. Yet, it is cool and fun, which makes it a great pastime game for girls and boys, but a game for adults as well. So, what are you waiting for? Download my virtual pet app and get a new funny cat that talks.<p>This Talking Cat is my virtual pet you will want to show to your friends. The tomcat Toby might seem mean, but neither you nor your friends will be able to resist the charm of this silly talking kitty. Once you start playing dress up games with the ginger cat, other talking animals, like talking parrot or dinosaur will be stacked somewhere in the far corner of your mind. Believe us, the meaner tiger cat and you will become best talking friends in a blink of an eye. <p>It is the cool app features that contribute to this game being a cool cat game for toddlers and becoming one of your favorites. Some of them are: <p>Dress up button- play dress up games and clothe your talking cat Toby according to your desires to make it look funny, fancy or elegant;<br>Talk to the tomcat and it will repeat everything you say in a funny voice;<br>Pet, poke and tickle the cat to make it jump, smile, or get angry. <p>Playing with talking cat friends is always fun; they tend to take animal games onto the next level. Not only will this ginger cat listen to you, but it will repeat what you say making it sound super cool. Once you add the silly outfit to the funny voice, Toby the cat that talks will become your mood maker for bad and good days all year around. Do not hesitate!
